                joint_names_.size(),
                collision_checking_enabled_ ? "enabled" : "disabled");
                
  } catch (const std::exception& e) {
    RCLCPP_ERROR(node_->get_logger(), "Initialization failed: %s", e.what());
    throw;
  }
}

WorkspaceSampler::SamplingResult WorkspaceSampler::computeBatchFK(
  const std::vector<std::vector<double>>& joint_samples,
  bool filter_collisions)
{
  SamplingResult result;
  auto start_time = std::chrono::high_resolution_clock::now();
  
  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(state_mutex_);
  
  result.poses.reserve(joint_samples.size());
  result.valid_indices.reserve(joint_samples.size());
  result.valid_joint_samples.reserve(joint_samples.size());
  
  for (size_t i = 0; i < joint_samples.size(); ++i)
  {
    const auto& sample = joint_samples[i];
    
    if (!validateJointSample(sample))
    {
      continue;
    }
    
    bool is_valid = true;
    
    // Check joint limits
    for (size_t j = 0; j < sample.size(); ++j)
    {
      if (sample[j] < joint_min_limits_[j] || sample[j] > joint_max_limits_[j])
      {
        is_valid = false;
        break;
      }
    }
    
    // Check collision if enabled and limits are satisfied
    if (is_valid && collision_checking_enabled_ && filter_collisions)
    {
      robot_state_->setJointGroupPositions(joint_model_group_, sample);
      robot_state_->update();
      is_valid = !planning_scene_->isStateColliding(*robot_state_, planning_group_);
    }
    
    if (is_valid || !filter_collisions)
    {
      // Compute FK
      robot_state_->setJointGroupPositions(joint_model_group_, sample);
      robot_state_->update();
      
      const Eigen::Isometry3d& end_effector_transform = 
        robot_state_->getGlobalLinkTransform(end_effector_link_);
      
      result.poses.push_back(eigenToRosPose(end_effector_transform));
      
      if (is_valid)
      {
        result.valid_indices.push_back(i);
        result.valid_joint_samples.push_back(sample);
      }
    }
  }
  
  auto end_time = std::chrono::high_resolution_clock::now();
  result.computation_time_ms = std::chrono::duration<double, std::milli>(end_time - start_time).count();
  
  if (!joint_samples.empty())
  {
    result.reachability_index = 100.0 * result.valid_indices.size() / joint_samples.size();
  }
  
  RCLCPP_DEBUG(node_->get_logger(),
               "Batch FK complete: %zu/%zu valid (%.1f%%) in %.2f ms",
               result.valid_indices.size(), joint_samples.size(),
               result.reachability_index, result.computation_time_ms);
  
  return result;
}

bool WorkspaceSampler::isStateValid(const std::vector<double>& joint_positions)
{
  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(state_mutex_);
  
  if (!validateJointSample(joint_positions))
  {
    return false;
  }
  
  // Check joint limits
  for (size_t i = 0; i < joint_positions.size(); ++i)
  {
    if (joint_positions[i] < joint_min_limits_[i] || 
        joint_positions[i] > joint_max_limits_[i])
    {
      return false;
    }
  }
  
  // Set state
  robot_state_->setJointGroupPositions(joint_model_group_, joint_positions);
  robot_state_->update();
  
  // Check collision if enabled
  if (collision_checking_enabled_)
  {
    return !planning_scene_->isStateColliding(*robot_state_, planning_group_);
  }
  
  return true;
}

std::pair<std::vector<double>, std::vector<double>> 
WorkspaceSampler::getJointLimits()
{
  return {joint_min_limits_, joint_max_limits_};
}

WorkspaceSampler::RobotInfo WorkspaceSampler::getRobotInfo() const
{
  RobotInfo info;
  info.planning_group = planning_group_;
  info.end_effector_link = end_effector_link_;
  info.joint_names = joint_names_;
  info.joint_min_limits = joint_min_limits_;
  info.joint_max_limits = joint_max_limits_;
  info.joint_velocity_limits = joint_velocity_limits_;
  info.num_joints = joint_names_.size();
  info.num_links = robot_model_->getLinkModelNames().size();
  info.collision_checking_available = true;
  
  // Get robot name from parameter or URDF
  node_->get_parameter_or("robot_name", info.robot_name, std::string("unknown"));
  
  // Get link names
  info.link_names = robot_model_->getLinkModelNames();
  
  // Get all group names
  info.group_names = robot_model_->getJointModelGroupNames();
  
  return info;
}

std::string WorkspaceSampler::getEndEffectorLink() const
{
  return end_effector_link_;
}

void WorkspaceSampler::setCollisionChecking(bool enable)
{
  collision_checking_enabled_ = enable;
  RCLCPP_INFO(node_->get_logger(), "Collision checking %s",
              enable ? "enabled" : "disabled");
}

size_t WorkspaceSampler::getJointCount() const
{
  return joint_names_.size();
}

std::vector<std::string> WorkspaceSampler::getJointNames() const
{
  return joint_names_;
}

bool WorkspaceSampler::setPlanningGroup(const std::string& group_name)
{
  const auto* new_group = robot_model_->getJointModelGroup(group_name);
  if (!new_group)
  {
    RCLCPP_ERROR(node_->get_logger(), "Planning group '%s' not found", group_name.c_str());
    return false;
  }
  
  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(state_mutex_);
  planning_group_ = group_name;
  joint_model_group_ = new_group;
  initializeJointLimits();
  
  // Update end-effector if not explicitly set
  if (end_effector_link_.empty() || 
      !robot_model_->hasLinkModel(end_effector_link_))
  {
    end_effector_link_ = findDefaultEndEffector();
  }
  
  RCLCPP_INFO(node_->get_logger(), "Switched to planning group: %s", group_name.c_str());
  return true;
}

std::vector<std::string> WorkspaceSampler::getAvailablePlanningGroups() const
{
  return robot_model_->getJointModelGroupNames();
}

bool WorkspaceSampler::saveRobotConfig(const std::string& filename) const
{
  try {
    YAML::Node config;
    config["robot_name"] = getRobotInfo().robot_name;
    config["planning_group"] = planning_group_;
    config["end_effector_link"] = end_effector_link_;
    config["joint_names"] = joint_names_;
    config["joint_min_limits"] = joint_min_limits_;
    config["joint_max_limits"] = joint_max_limits_;
    config["joint_velocity_limits"] = joint_velocity_limits_;
    
    std::ofstream fout(filename);
    fout << config;
    return true;
  } catch (const std::exception& e) {
    RCLCPP_ERROR(node_->get_logger(), "Failed to save config: %s", e.what());
    return false;
  }
}

bool WorkspaceSampler::loadRobotConfig(const std::string& filename)
{
  try {
    YAML::Node config = YAML::LoadFile(filename);
    
    // Only load configuration, actual robot model must already be loaded
    if (config["planning_group"])
    {
      setPlanningGroup(config["planning_group"].as<std::string>());
    }
    
    return true;
  } catch (const std::exception& e) {
    RCLCPP_ERROR(node_->get_logger(), "Failed to load config: %s", e.what());
    return false;
  }
}

geometry_msgs::msg::Pose 
WorkspaceSampler::eigenToRosPose(const Eigen::Isometry3d& eigen_pose)
{
  geometry_msgs::msg::Pose pose;
  
  pose.position.x = eigen_pose.translation().x();
  pose.position.y = eigen_pose.translation().y();
  pose.position.z = eigen_pose.translation().z();
  
  Eigen::Quaterniond quat(eigen_pose.rotation());
  pose.orientation.w = quat.w();
  pose.orientation.x = quat.x();
  pose.orientation.y = quat.y();
  pose.orientation.z = quat.z();
  
  return pose;
}

bool WorkspaceSampler::validateJointSample(const std::vector<double>& sample)
{
  if (sample.size() != joint_names_.size())
  {
    RCLCPP_WARN(node_->get_logger(), 
                "Joint sample size mismatch. Expected %zu, got %zu.",
                joint_names_.size(), sample.size());
    return false;
  }
  return true;
}

void WorkspaceSampler::initializeJointLimits()
{
  joint_min_limits_.clear();
  joint_max_limits_.clear();
  joint_velocity_limits_.clear();
  joint_names_.clear();
  
  const auto& joint_models = joint_model_group_->getJointModels();
  for (const auto& joint : joint_models)
  {
    if (joint->getType() == moveit::core::JointModel::REVOLUTE ||
        joint->getType() == moveit::core::JointModel::PRISMATIC)
    {
      const auto* bounds = joint->getVariableBounds();
      joint_min_limits_.push_back(bounds->min_position_);
      joint_max_limits_.push_back(bounds->max_position_);
      joint_velocity_limits_.push_back(bounds->max_velocity_);
      joint_names_.push_back(joint->getName());
    }
  }
}

std::string WorkspaceSampler::findDefaultEndEffector() const
{
  const auto& link_names = joint_model_group_->getLinkModelNames();
  if (!link_names.empty())
  {
    return link_names.back();
  }
  return "";
}

} // namespace autocert_core

===== FILE: ./autocert_core/src/collision_checker.cpp =====
#include "autocert_core/collision_checker.hpp"
#include <moveit/robot_state/robot_state.h>

namespace autocert_core
{

CollisionChecker::CollisionChecker(
  std::shared_ptr<planning_scene::PlanningScene> planning_scene,
  const std::string& group_name)
: planning_scene_(planning_scene),
  group_name_(group_name)
{
  robot_state_ = std::make_unique<moveit::core::RobotState>(
    planning_scene_->getRobotModel());
  joint_model_group_ = planning_scene_->getRobotModel()->getJointModelGroup(group_name);
}

bool CollisionChecker::checkState(const std::vector<double>& joint_positions)
{
  robot_state_->setJointGroupPositions(joint_model_group_, joint_positions);
  robot_state_->update();
  
  return !planning_scene_->isStateColliding(*robot_state_, group_name_);
}

std::vector<bool> CollisionChecker::batchCheck(
  const std::vector<std::vector<double>>& joint_samples)
{
  std::vector<bool> results;
  results.reserve(joint_samples.size());
  
  for (const auto& sample : joint_samples)
  {
    results.push_back(checkState(sample));
  }
  
  return results;
}

} // namespace autocert_core

===== FILE: ./autocert_core/include/autocert_core/workspace_sampler.hpp =====
#ifndef AUTOCERT_CORE__WORKSPACE_SAMPLER_HPP_
#define AUTOCERT_CORE__WORKSPACE_SAMPLER_HPP_

#include <rclcpp/rclcpp.hpp>
#include <moveit/robot_model/robot_model.h>
#include <moveit/robot_state/robot_state.h>
#include <moveit/planning_scene/planning_scene.h>
#include <geometry_msgs/msg/pose.hpp>
#include <geometry_msgs/msg/pose_array.hpp>
#include <vector>
#include <string>
#include <memory>
#include <mutex>
#include <Eigen/Geometry>
#include <yaml-cpp/yaml.h>

namespace autocert_core
{

/**
 * @brief Core workspace sampling engine using MoveIt2 low-level APIs
 * 
 * This class provides high-performance forward kinematics computation
 * for batches of joint configurations with optional collision checking.
 * It is designed to be robot-agnostic and thread-safe.
 */
class WorkspaceSampler
{
public:
  /**
   * @brief Robot information structure
   */
  struct RobotInfo
  {
    std::string robot_name;
    std::string planning_group;
    std::string end_effector_link;
    std::vector<std::string> joint_names;
    std::vector<std::string> link_names;
    std::vector<double> joint_min_limits;
    std::vector<double> joint_max_limits;
    std::vector<double> joint_velocity_limits;
    size_t num_joints;
    size_t num_links;
    bool collision_checking_available;
  };

  /**
   * @brief Sampling result structure
   */
  struct SamplingResult
  {
    std::vector<geometry_msgs::msg::Pose> poses;
    std::vector<size_t> valid_indices;
    std::vector<std::vector<double>> valid_joint_samples;
    double computation_time_ms;
    double reachability_index;
  };

  /**
   * @brief Constructor
   * @param node ROS2 node for logging and parameters
   * @param robot_description Robot description parameter name (default: "robot_description")
   */
  explicit WorkspaceSampler(
    rclcpp::Node::SharedPtr node,
    const std::string& robot_description = "robot_description");
  
  /**
   * @brief Destructor
   */
  ~WorkspaceSampler() = default;

  /**
   * @brief Compute forward kinematics for a batch of joint samples
   * @param joint_samples Vector of joint configurations (each inner vector is a joint state)
   * @param filter_collisions Whether to filter out colliding configurations
   * @return SamplingResult containing poses and validity information
   */
  SamplingResult computeBatchFK(
    const std::vector<std::vector<double>>& joint_samples,
    bool filter_collisions = true);

  /**
   * @brief Check if a joint configuration is valid (within limits and collision-free)
   * @param joint_positions Joint configuration to check
   * @return True if configuration is valid
   */
  bool isStateValid(const std::vector<double>& joint_positions);

  /**
   * @brief Get joint limits for the robot
   * @return Pair of vectors (min_limits, max_limits)
   */
  std::pair<std::vector<double>, std::vector<double>> getJointLimits();

  /**
   * @brief Get comprehensive robot information
   * @return RobotInfo structure
   */
  RobotInfo getRobotInfo() const;

  /**
   * @brief Get the end-effector link name
   * @return End-effector link name
   */
  std::string getEndEffectorLink() const;

  /**
   * @brief Enable/disable collision checking
   * @param enable True to enable collision checking
   */
  void setCollisionChecking(bool enable);

  /**
   * @brief Get collision checking status
   * @return True if collision checking is enabled
   */
  bool getCollisionChecking() const { return collision_checking_enabled_; }

  /**
   * @brief Get number of joints in the group
   * @return Joint count
   */
  size_t getJointCount() const;

  /**
   * @brief Get joint names in the group
   * @return Vector of joint names
   */
  std::vector<std::string> getJointNames() const;

  /**
   * @brief Set planning group by name
   * @param group_name Name of the planning group
   * @return True if successful
   */
  bool setPlanningGroup(const std::string& group_name);

  /**
   * @brief Get available planning groups
   * @return Vector of planning group names
   */
  std::vector<std::string> getAvailablePlanningGroups() const;

  /**
   * @brief Save robot configuration to YAML
   * @param filename Output filename
   * @return True if successful
   */
  bool saveRobotConfig(const std::string& filename) const;

  /**
   * @brief Load robot configuration from YAML
   * @param filename Input filename
   * @return True if successful
   */
  bool loadRobotConfig(const std::string& filename);

private:
  rclcpp::Node::SharedPtr node_;
  moveit::core::RobotModelPtr robot_model_;
  std::unique_ptr<moveit::core::RobotState> robot_state_;
  std::unique_ptr<planning_scene::PlanningScene> planning_scene_;
  std::unique_ptr<robot_model_loader::RobotModelLoader> model_loader_;
  
  std::string planning_group_;
  std::string end_effector_link_;
  const moveit::core::JointModelGroup* joint_model_group_;
  
  std::vector<double> joint_min_limits_;
  std::vector<double> joint_max_limits_;
  std::vector<double> joint_velocity_limits_;
  std::vector<std::string> joint_names_;
  
  bool collision_checking_enabled_;
  mutable std::mutex state_mutex_;
  
  /**
   * @brief Convert Eigen transform to ROS pose message
   */
  geometry_msgs::msg::Pose eigenToRosPose(const Eigen::Isometry3d& eigen_pose);

  /**
   * @brief Validate joint sample size and limits
   */
  bool validateJointSample(const std::vector<double>& sample);

  /**
   * @brief Initialize joint limits from model
   */
  void initializeJointLimits();

  /**
   * @brief Find default end-effector link
   */
  std::string findDefaultEndEffector() const;
};

} // namespace autocert_core

#endif // AUTOCERT_CORE__WORKSPACE_SAMPLER_HPP_

===== FILE: ./autocert_core/src/batch_fk_server.cpp =====
#include <rclcpp/rclcpp.hpp>
#include <autocert_interfaces/srv/batch_fk.hpp>
#include <autocert_interfaces/srv/get_joint_limits.hpp>
#include <autocert_interfaces/srv/get_robot_info.hpp>
#include <autocert_interfaces/srv/check_collision.hpp>
#include <autocert_interfaces/srv/sample_workspace.hpp>
#include "autocert_core/workspace_sampler.hpp"
#include <memory>
#include <string>
#include <span>
#include <Eigen/Core>
#include <atomic>
#include <chrono>
#include <algorithm>

namespace autocert
{

class BatchFKServer : public rclcpp::Node
{
public:
  BatchFKServer() : Node("batch_fk_server")
  {
    // Declare parameters with defaults - use int for all numeric parameters
    this->declare_parameter<std::string>("robot_description_param", "robot_description");
    this->declare_parameter<std::string>("planning_group", "");
    this->declare_parameter<std::string>("end_effector_link", "");
    this->declare_parameter<bool>("enable_collision_checking", true);
    this->declare_parameter<int>("service_threads", 4);
    this->declare_parameter<bool>("enable_performance_logging", false);
    this->declare_parameter<int>("max_samples_per_request", 100000);
    this->declare_parameter<int>("response_chunk_size", 20000);
    
    RCLCPP_INFO(this->get_logger(), 
                "BatchFKServer created in namespace '%s' - v2.0.0, waiting for parameters...",
                this->get_namespace());
    
    // Use a timer to initialize after parameters are loaded
    init_timer_ = this->create_wall_timer(
      std::chrono::milliseconds(500),
      std::bind(&BatchFKServer::initialize, this));
  }
  
  void initialize()
  {
    // Cancel the timer so this only runs once
    init_timer_->cancel();
    
    RCLCPP_INFO(this->get_logger(), "Initializing BatchFKServer...");
    
    try {
      // Get the parameter NAME (default: "robot_description")
      std::string robot_description_param = this->get_parameter("robot_description_param").as_string();
      
      RCLCPP_INFO(this->get_logger(), "Looking for robot description in parameter: '%s'", 
                  robot_description_param.c_str());
      
      // List all parameters for debugging
      auto param_names = this->list_parameters({}, 10);
      RCLCPP_INFO(this->get_logger(), "Available parameters (%zu):", param_names.names.size());
      for (const auto& name : param_names.names) {
        RCLCPP_INFO(this->get_logger(), "  - %s", name.c_str());
      }
      
      // Get the actual robot description
      std::string robot_description_xml;
      if (!this->get_parameter(robot_description_param, robot_description_xml)) {
        RCLCPP_ERROR(this->get_logger(), 
                     "Parameter '%s' not found!",
                     robot_description_param.c_str());
        
        // Special handling for command-line parameters
        if (this->has_parameter("robot_description")) {
          RCLCPP_INFO(this->get_logger(), "Found 'robot_description' parameter directly!");
          robot_description_xml = this->get_parameter("robot_description").as_string();
        } else {
          throw std::runtime_error("Robot description parameter not found");
        }
      }
      
      if (robot_description_xml.empty()) {
        RCLCPP_ERROR(this->get_logger(), 
                     "Parameter '%s' is empty!",
                     robot_description_param.c_str());
        throw std::runtime_error("Robot description parameter is empty");
      }
      
      RCLCPP_INFO(this->get_logger(), 
                  "Robot description loaded from param '%s' (%zu chars)", 
                  robot_description_param.c_str(),
                  robot_description_xml.length());
      
      // Get other parameters
      std::string planning_group = this->get_parameter("planning_group").as_string();
      bool enable_collision = this->get_parameter("enable_collision_checking").as_bool();
      max_samples_per_request_ = this->get_parameter("max_samples_per_request").as_int();
      response_chunk_size_ = this->get_parameter("response_chunk_size").as_int();
      enable_performance_logging_ = this->get_parameter("enable_performance_logging").as_bool();
      
      RCLCPP_INFO(this->get_logger(), 
                  "Parameters: planning_group='%s', collision=%s, max_samples=%d, chunk=%d",
                  planning_group.c_str(),
                  enable_collision ? "true" : "false",
                  max_samples_per_request_,
                  response_chunk_size_);
      
      // Create sampler with shared_ptr
      sampler_ = std::make_unique<autocert_core::WorkspaceSampler>(
          shared_from_this(),
          robot_description_param
      );
      
      // Set planning group if specified
      if (!planning_group.empty()) {
        sampler_->setPlanningGroup(planning_group);
      }
      
      // Set end effector link if specified
      std::string end_effector_link = this->get_parameter("end_effector_link").as_string();
      if (!end_effector_link.empty()) {
        sampler_->setEndEffectorLink(end_effector_link);
      }
      
      // Set collision checking
      sampler_->setCollisionChecking(enable_collision);
      
      RCLCPP_INFO(this->get_logger(), "WorkspaceSampler initialized successfully");
      
      // Get robot info for logging
      auto info = sampler_->getRobotInfo();
      RCLCPP_INFO(this->get_logger(), 
                  "Robot: '%s' | Group: '%s' | Joints: %zu | Links: %zu",
                  info.robot_name.c_str(), 
                  info.planning_group.c_str(), 
                  info.num_joints,
                  info.num_links);
      
      // Create services
      createServices();
      
      RCLCPP_INFO(this->get_logger(), "BatchFKServer fully initialized and ready");
      
    } catch (const std::exception& e) {
      RCLCPP_ERROR(this->get_logger(), "Initialization failed: %s", e.what());
      // Don't throw - let the node continue running (services won't work)
    }
  }
  
  // Public accessors for main()
  size_t getTotalRequests() const { return total_requests_.load(); }
  size_t getTotalSamplesProcessed() const { return total_samples_processed_.load(); }

private:
  void createServices()
  {
    RCLCPP_INFO(this->get_logger(), "Creating services...");
    
    fk_srv_ = this->create_service<autocert_interfaces::srv::BatchFK>(
      "batch_fk",
      std::bind(&BatchFKServer::handleBatchFK, this,
                std::placeholders::_1, std::placeholders::_2));
    
    limits_srv_ = this->create_service<autocert_interfaces::srv::GetJointLimits>(
      "get_joint_limits",
      std::bind(&BatchFKServer::handleGetLimits, this,
                std::placeholders::_1, std::placeholders::_2));
    
    info_srv_ = this->create_service<autocert_interfaces::srv::GetRobotInfo>(
      "get_robot_info",
      std::bind(&BatchFKServer::handleGetInfo, this,
                std::placeholders::_1, std::placeholders::_2));
    
    collision_srv_ = this->create_service<autocert_interfaces::srv::CheckCollision>(
      "check_collision",
      std::bind(&BatchFKServer::handleCheckCollision, this,
                std::placeholders::_1, std::placeholders::_2));
    
    sample_srv_ = this->create_service<autocert_interfaces::srv::SampleWorkspace>(
      "sample_workspace",
      std::bind(&BatchFKServer::handleSampleWorkspace, this,
                std::placeholders::_1, std::placeholders::_2));
    
    RCLCPP_INFO(this->get_logger(), "All services created and ready");
  }
  
  void handleBatchFK(
    const std::shared_ptr<autocert_interfaces::srv::BatchFK::Request> request,
    std::shared_ptr<autocert_interfaces::srv::BatchFK::Response> response)
  {
    // Check if sampler is initialized
    if (!sampler_) {
      RCLCPP_ERROR(this->get_logger(), "Sampler not initialized!");
      response->error_code = 4;
      response->error_message = "Sampler not initialized";
      return;
    }
    
    // Initialize response with success
    response->error_code = 0;
    response->error_message = "";
    
    // ENFORCE max chunk size - reject requests that are too large
    if (request->num_samples > response_chunk_size_) {
      RCLCPP_ERROR(this->get_logger(), 
                   "Request too large: %d samples (max chunk: %d). Please split into smaller batches.",
                   request->num_samples, response_chunk_size_);
      
      response->error_code = 1;
      response->error_message = "Request too large. Max samples per request: " + 
                                std::to_string(response_chunk_size_);
      return;
    }
    
    // Also check absolute maximum
    if (request->num_samples > max_samples_per_request_) {
      RCLCPP_ERROR(this->get_logger(), 
                   "Request exceeds absolute maximum: %d > %d",
                   request->num_samples, max_samples_per_request_);
      response->error_code = 2;
      response->error_message = "Request exceeds absolute maximum";
      return;
    }
    
    if (enable_performance_logging_) {
      RCLCPP_INFO(this->get_logger(), 
                  "Batch FK: %d samples, %d joints",
                  request->num_samples, request->num_joints);
    }
    
    // Validate input size
    size_t expected_size = static_cast<size_t>(request->num_samples) * request->num_joints;
    if (request->joint_samples.size() != expected_size) {
      RCLCPP_ERROR(this->get_logger(), 
                   "Invalid input size: expected %zu, got %zu",
                   expected_size, request->joint_samples.size());
      response->error_code = 3;
      response->error_message = "Invalid input size";
      return;
    }
    
    const double* data_ptr = request->joint_samples.data();
    const size_t num_joints = request->num_joints;
    const size_t num_samples = request->num_samples;
    const bool filter_collisions = request->filter_collisions;
    
    // Pre-allocate joint_values vector (reused for all samples - zero allocations!)
    std::vector<double> joint_values(num_joints);
    
    // Pre-allocate response vectors with capacity
    response->poses.reserve(num_samples);
    response->valid_indices.reserve(num_samples);
    
    auto start_time = std::chrono::steady_clock::now();
    
    // Process all samples with zero allocations per sample
    for (size_t i = 0; i < num_samples; ++i) {
      // Copy data to vector (temporary allocation but necessary for API)
      for (size_t j = 0; j < num_joints; ++j) {
        joint_values[j] = data_ptr[i * num_joints + j];
      }
      
      // Compute FK using the vector
      auto pose = sampler_->computeFK(joint_values);
      response->poses.push_back(pose);
      
      // Check validity if needed
      bool is_valid = true;
      if (filter_collisions) {
        is_valid = sampler_->isStateValid(joint_values);
      }
      
      if (is_valid) {
        response->valid_indices.push_back(static_cast<int>(i));
      }
    }
    
    auto end_time = std::chrono::steady_clock::now();
    double computation_time = std::chrono::duration<double, std::milli>(end_time - start_time).count();
    
    response->end_effector_link = sampler_->getEndEffectorLink();
    response->computation_time_ms.push_back(computation_time);
    
    // Increment counters
    total_requests_++;
    total_samples_processed_ += num_samples;
    
    // Log performance occasionally
    if (enable_performance_logging_ || total_requests_ % 100 == 0) {
      double reachability = (response->valid_indices.size() * 100.0) / num_samples;
      double avg_time_per_sample = computation_time / num_samples;
      RCLCPP_INFO(this->get_logger(), 
                  "FK complete: %zu/%zu valid (%.1f%%) in %.2f ms (%.3f ms/sample) | Total: %zu req, %zu samples",
                  response->valid_indices.size(), 
                  num_samples,
                  reachability,
                  computation_time,
                  avg_time_per_sample,
                  total_requests_.load(),
                  total_samples_processed_.load());
    }
  }
  
  void handleGetLimits(
    const std::shared_ptr<autocert_interfaces::srv::GetJointLimits::Request> request,
    std::shared_ptr<autocert_interfaces::srv::GetJointLimits::Response> response)
  {
    (void)request;
    
    if (!sampler_) {
      RCLCPP_ERROR(this->get_logger(), "Sampler not initialized!");
      return;
    }
    
    auto limits = sampler_->getJointLimits();
    auto info = sampler_->getRobotInfo();
    
    response->joint_names = info.joint_names;
    response->min_limits = limits.first;
    response->max_limits = limits.second;
    response->planning_group = info.planning_group;
    response->end_effector_link = info.end_effector_link;
    response->num_joints = static_cast<int32_t>(info.num_joints);
    response->velocity_limits = info.joint_velocity_limits;
    response->acceleration_limits = std::vector<double>(info.num_joints, 0.0);
    
    RCLCPP_DEBUG(this->get_logger(), "Returning joint limits for %zu joints", 
                 info.num_joints);
  }
  
  void handleGetInfo(
    const std::shared_ptr<autocert_interfaces::srv::GetRobotInfo::Request> request,
    std::shared_ptr<autocert_interfaces::srv::GetRobotInfo::Response> response)
  {
    (void)request;
    
    if (!sampler_) {
      RCLCPP_ERROR(this->get_logger(), "Sampler not initialized!");
      return;
    }
    
    auto info = sampler_->getRobotInfo();
    
    response->robot_name = info.robot_name;
    response->planning_group = info.planning_group;
    response->end_effector_link = info.end_effector_link;
    response->joint_names = info.joint_names;
    response->link_names = info.link_names;
    response->group_names = info.group_names;
    response->joint_min_limits = info.joint_min_limits;
    response->joint_max_limits = info.joint_max_limits;
    response->joint_velocity_limits = info.joint_velocity_limits;
    response->num_joints = static_cast<int32_t>(info.num_joints);
    response->num_links = static_cast<int32_t>(info.num_links);
    response->collision_checking_available = true;
    response->kinematics_solver_available = true;
    response->kinematics_solver_name = "builtin";
    response->default_timeout = 10.0;
    
    RCLCPP_DEBUG(this->get_logger(), "Returning robot info for '%s'", 
                 info.robot_name.c_str());
  }
  
  void handleCheckCollision(
    const std::shared_ptr<autocert_interfaces::srv::CheckCollision::Request> request,
    std::shared_ptr<autocert_interfaces::srv::CheckCollision::Response> response)
  {
    if (!sampler_) {
      RCLCPP_ERROR(this->get_logger(), "Sampler not initialized!");
      return;
    }
    
    // Convert to vector for isStateValid
    std::vector<double> joint_positions(
      request->joint_positions.begin(),
      request->joint_positions.end()
    );
    
    bool is_valid = sampler_->isStateValid(joint_positions);
    response->in_collision = !is_valid;
    response->self_collision = false;
    response->environment_collision = !is_valid;
    
    RCLCPP_DEBUG(this->get_logger(), "Collision check: %s",
                 is_valid ? "valid" : "in collision");
  }
  
  void handleSampleWorkspace(
    const std::shared_ptr<autocert_interfaces::srv::SampleWorkspace::Request> request,
    std::shared_ptr<autocert_interfaces::srv::SampleWorkspace::Response> response)
  {
    RCLCPP_INFO(this->get_logger(), 
                "Workspace sampling request: %d samples, strategy: %s",
                request->num_samples, request->sampling_strategy.c_str());
    
    response->reachability_index = 0.0;
    response->workspace_volume = 0.0;
    
    RCLCPP_WARN_ONCE(this->get_logger(), 
                     "SampleWorkspace is a placeholder - use Python client");
  }
  
  // Timer for delayed initialization
  rclcpp::TimerBase::SharedPtr init_timer_;
  
  std::unique_ptr<autocert_core::WorkspaceSampler> sampler_;
  rclcpp::Service<autocert_interfaces::srv::BatchFK>::SharedPtr fk_srv_;
  rclcpp::Service<autocert_interfaces::srv::GetJointLimits>::SharedPtr limits_srv_;
  rclcpp::Service<autocert_interfaces::srv::GetRobotInfo>::SharedPtr info_srv_;
  rclcpp::Service<autocert_interfaces::srv::CheckCollision>::SharedPtr collision_srv_;
  rclcpp::Service<autocert_interfaces::srv::SampleWorkspace>::SharedPtr sample_srv_;
  
  // Performance monitoring
  std::atomic<size_t> total_requests_{0};
  std::atomic<size_t> total_samples_processed_{0};
  int max_samples_per_request_{100000};
  int response_chunk_size_{20000};
  bool enable_performance_logging_{false};
};

} // namespace autocert

int main(int argc, char** argv)
{
  rclcpp::init(argc, argv);
  
  auto node = std::make_shared<autocert::BatchFKServer>();
  
  // Use multi-threaded executor
  int service_threads = 4;  // Default
  try {
    service_threads = node->get_parameter("service_threads").as_int();
  } catch (...) {
    // Parameter not available yet, use default
  }
  
  rclcpp::executors::MultiThreadedExecutor executor(
    rclcpp::ExecutorOptions(), 
    service_threads
  );
  executor.add_node(node);
  
  RCLCPP_INFO(node->get_logger(), "Batch FK server running with multi-threaded executor");
  executor.spin();
  
  // Final statistics
  RCLCPP_INFO(node->get_logger(), 
              "Shutting down. Processed %zu total requests, %zu samples",
              node->getTotalRequests(),
              node->getTotalSamplesProcessed());
  
  rclcpp::shutdown();
  return 0;
}

===== FILE: ./autocert_core/src/workspace_sampler.cpp =====
#include "autocert_core/workspace_sampler.hpp"
#include <moveit/robot_state/conversions.h>
#include <Eigen/Geometry>
#include <algorithm>
#include <chrono>

namespace autocert_core
{

WorkspaceSampler::WorkspaceSampler(
  const rclcpp::Node::SharedPtr& node,
  const std::string& robot_description_param)
: node_(node)
, joint_model_group_(nullptr)
, collision_checking_enabled_(false)
{
  auto logger = node_->get_logger();
  RCLCPP_INFO(logger, "Initializing WorkspaceSampler with param: %s", 
              robot_description_param.c_str());
  
  try {
    // Load robot model using the parameter NAME
    model_loader_ = std::make_shared<robot_model_loader::RobotModelLoader>(
      node_, robot_description_param, true);
    
    robot_model_ = model_loader_->getModel();
    if (!robot_model_)
    {
      RCLCPP_ERROR(logger, "Failed to load robot model from param '%s'", 
                   robot_description_param.c_str());
      throw std::runtime_error("Failed to load robot model");
    }
    
    // Create base planning scene (for cloning - thread-safe)
    base_planning_scene_ = std::make_shared<planning_scene::PlanningScene>(robot_model_);
    
    // Get first available group as default
    const auto& group_names = robot_model_->getJointModelGroupNames();
    if (group_names.empty())
    {
      RCLCPP_ERROR(logger, "No joint model groups found");
      throw std::runtime_error("No joint model groups found");
    }
    
    planning_group_ = group_names[0];
    joint_model_group_ = robot_model_->getJointModelGroup(planning_group_);
    if (!joint_model_group_)
    {
      RCLCPP_ERROR(logger, "Failed to get joint model group");
      throw std::runtime_error("Failed to get joint model group");
    }
    
    // Find default end effector from group
    end_effector_link_ = findDefaultEndEffector();
    
    // Initialize joint limits
    initializeJointLimits();
    
    // Increment version to initialize thread-local data
    state_version_++;
    
    RCLCPP_INFO(logger, 
                "WorkspaceSampler initialized:\n"
                "  Planning group: %s\n"
                "  End-effector: %s\n"
                "  Joints: %zu",
                planning_group_.c_str(),
                end_effector_link_.c_str(),
                joint_names_.size());
                
  } catch (const std::exception& e) {
    RCLCPP_ERROR(logger, "Initialization failed: %s", e.what());
    throw;
  }
}

WorkspaceSampler::~WorkspaceSampler()
{
  // Nothing to do
}

WorkspaceSampler::ThreadLocalData* WorkspaceSampler::getThreadLocalData()
{
  thread_local static std::unique_ptr<ThreadLocalData> thread_data;
  thread_local static uint64_t last_version = 0;
  
  uint64_t current_version = state_version_.load(std::memory_order_acquire);
  
  // Check if thread data needs to be recreated due to group change
  if (!thread_data || last_version != current_version)
  {
    auto new_data = std::make_unique<ThreadLocalData>();
    
    // Create thread-local robot state
    new_data->robot_state = std::make_unique<moveit::core::RobotState>(robot_model_);
    new_data->robot_state->setToDefaultValues();
    
    // Create thread-local planning scene (clone of base scene)
    if (base_planning_scene_) {
      new_data->planning_scene = base_planning_scene_->diff();
    }
    
    // Configure collision request (once per thread)
    new_data->collision_request.contacts = false;
    new_data->collision_request.max_contacts = 1;
    new_data->collision_request.max_contacts_per_pair = 1;
    new_data->collision_request.verbose = false;
    
    new_data->version = current_version;
    
    thread_data = std::move(new_data);
    last_version = current_version;
  }
  
  return thread_data.get();
}

void WorkspaceSampler::setPlanningGroup(const std::string& group_name)
{
  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);
  
  const auto* group = robot_model_->getJointModelGroup(group_name);
  if (!group) {
    RCLCPP_ERROR(node_->get_logger(), 
                 "Planning group '%s' not found", group_name.c_str());
    return;
  }
  
  planning_group_ = group_name;
  joint_model_group_ = group;
  
  // Update end effector from new group
  end_effector_link_ = findDefaultEndEffector();
  
  // Invalidate cached info
  info_cached_ = false;
  
  // Re-initialize joint limits for new group
  initializeJointLimits();
  
  // Increment version to invalidate thread-local states
  state_version_++;
  
  RCLCPP_INFO(node_->get_logger(), 
              "Switched to planning group: %s (version: %llu)", 
              group_name.c_str(), state_version_.load());
}

void WorkspaceSampler::setEndEffectorLink(const std::string& link_name)
{
  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);
  
  if (robot_model_->hasLinkModel(link_name)) {
    end_effector_link_ = link_name;
    info_cached_ = false;
    
    // Increment version to update thread-local data
    state_version_++;
    
    RCLCPP_INFO(node_->get_logger(), "End effector set to: %s", link_name.c_str());
  } else {
    RCLCPP_ERROR(node_->get_logger(), 
                 "Link '%s' not found", link_name.c_str());
  }
}

void WorkspaceSampler::setCollisionChecking(bool enable)
{
  collision_checking_enabled_ = enable;
}

RobotInfo WorkspaceSampler::getRobotInfo() const
{
  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);
  
  if (info_cached_) {
    return cached_info_;
  }
  
  RobotInfo info;
  info.robot_name = robot_model_->getName();
  info.planning_group = planning_group_;
  info.end_effector_link = end_effector_link_;
  info.joint_names = joint_names_;
  info.joint_min_limits = joint_min_limits_;
  info.joint_max_limits = joint_max_limits_;
  info.joint_velocity_limits = joint_velocity_limits_;
  info.num_joints = joint_names_.size();
  
  // Get link names
  const auto& link_models = robot_model_->getLinkModels();
  info.link_names.reserve(link_models.size());
  for (const auto& link : link_models) {
    info.link_names.push_back(link->getName());
  }
  info.num_links = info.link_names.size();
  
  // Get group names
  info.group_names = robot_model_->getJointModelGroupNames();
  
  cached_info_ = info;
  info_cached_ = true;
  
  return info;
}

std::pair<std::vector<double>, std::vector<double>> WorkspaceSampler::getJointLimits() const
{
  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);
  return {joint_min_limits_, joint_max_limits_};
}

geometry_msgs::msg::Pose WorkspaceSampler::computeFK(const std::vector<double>& joint_values)
{
  if (!joint_model_group_) {
    throw std::runtime_error("No planning group set");
  }
  
  // Use active variable count (handles mimic joints correctly)
  if (joint_values.size() != joint_model_group_->getActiveVariableCount()) {
    throw std::runtime_error("Invalid number of joint values");
  }
  
  // Get thread-local data
  auto* local_data = getThreadLocalData();
  auto* state = local_data->robot_state.get();
  
  // Set joint positions
  state->setJointGroupPositions(joint_model_group_, joint_values);
  state->update();
  
  // Get end effector transform
  const Eigen::Isometry3d& end_effector_state = 
      state->getGlobalLinkTransform(end_effector_link_);
  
  // Convert to ROS pose message
  geometry_msgs::msg::Pose pose;
  pose.position.x = end_effector_state.translation().x();
  pose.position.y = end_effector_state.translation().y();
  pose.position.z = end_effector_state.translation().z();
  
  Eigen::Quaterniond quat(end_effector_state.rotation());
  pose.orientation.x = quat.x();
  pose.orientation.y = quat.y();
  pose.orientation.z = quat.z();
  pose.orientation.w = quat.w();
  
  return pose;
}

BatchFKResult WorkspaceSampler::computeBatchFK(
  const std::vector<std::vector<double>>& joint_samples,
  bool filter_collisions)
{
  BatchFKResult result;
  auto start_time = std::chrono::steady_clock::now();
  
  // Pre-allocate vectors
  result.poses.reserve(joint_samples.size());
  result.valid_indices.reserve(joint_samples.size());
  
  // Get thread-local data
  auto* local_data = getThreadLocalData();
  auto* state = local_data->robot_state.get();
  
  for (size_t i = 0; i < joint_samples.size(); ++i) {
    const auto& sample = joint_samples[i];
    
    // Set joint positions
    state->setJointGroupPositions(joint_model_group_, sample);
    state->update();
    
    // Get end effector transform
    const Eigen::Isometry3d& end_effector_state = 
        state->getGlobalLinkTransform(end_effector_link_);
    
    // Convert to pose
    geometry_msgs::msg::Pose pose;
    pose.position.x = end_effector_state.translation().x();
    pose.position.y = end_effector_state.translation().y();
    pose.position.z = end_effector_state.translation().z();
    
    Eigen::Quaterniond quat(end_effector_state.rotation());
    pose.orientation.x = quat.x();
    pose.orientation.y = quat.y();
    pose.orientation.z = quat.z();
    pose.orientation.w = quat.w();
    
    result.poses.emplace_back(std::move(pose));
    
    // Check collision if requested
    if (filter_collisions && collision_checking_enabled_) {
      // Use thread-local planning scene for collision checking
      if (local_data->planning_scene) {
        // Reset result for reuse
        local_data->collision_result.clear();
        
        local_data->planning_scene->checkCollision(
          local_data->collision_request, 
          local_data->collision_result, 
          *state
        );
        
        if (!local_data->collision_result.collision) {
          result.valid_indices.push_back(static_cast<int>(i));
        }
      } else {
        result.valid_indices.push_back(static_cast<int>(i));
      }
    } else {
      result.valid_indices.push_back(static_cast<int>(i));
    }
  }
  
  auto end_time = std::chrono::steady_clock::now();
  result.computation_time_ms = std::chrono::duration<double, std::milli>(
    end_time - start_time).count();
  
  result.reachability_index = (result.valid_indices.size() * 100.0) / joint_samples.size();
  
  return result;
}

bool WorkspaceSampler::isStateValid(const std::vector<double>& joint_values)
{
  if (!collision_checking_enabled_) {
    return true;
  }
  
  // Get thread-local data
  auto* local_data = getThreadLocalData();
  auto* state = local_data->robot_state.get();
  
  // Set joint positions
  state->setJointGroupPositions(joint_model_group_, joint_values);
  state->update();
  
  // Check collision using thread-local planning scene
  if (local_data->planning_scene) {
    // Reset result for reuse
    local_data->collision_result.clear();
    
    local_data->planning_scene->checkCollision(
      local_data->collision_request, 
      local_data->collision_result, 
      *state
    );
    
    return !local_data->collision_result.collision;
  }
  
  return true;
}

std::string WorkspaceSampler::findDefaultEndEffector() const
{
  if (!joint_model_group_) {
    return "";
  }
  
  // Get the last link in the kinematic chain of the group
  const auto& link_names = joint_model_group_->getLinkModelNames();
  if (!link_names.empty()) {
    return link_names.back();
  }
  
  return "";
}

void WorkspaceSampler::initializeJointLimits()
{
  joint_min_limits_.clear();
  joint_max_limits_.clear();
  joint_velocity_limits_.clear();
  joint_names_.clear();
  
  if (!joint_model_group_) return;
  
  const auto& joints = joint_model_group_->getJointModels();
  for (const auto& joint : joints)
  {
    if (joint->getType() == moveit::core::JointModel::REVOLUTE ||
        joint->getType() == moveit::core::JointModel::PRISMATIC)
    {
      const auto& bounds = joint->getVariableBounds();
      if (!bounds.empty()) {
        joint_min_limits_.push_back(bounds[0].min_position_);
        joint_max_limits_.push_back(bounds[0].max_position_);
        joint_velocity_limits_.push_back(bounds[0].max_velocity_);
        joint_names_.push_back(joint->getName());
      }
    }
  }
}

} // namespace autocert_core

===== FILE: ./autocert_core/src/collision_checker.cpp =====
#include "autocert_core/collision_checker.hpp"
#include <moveit/robot_state/robot_state.h>

namespace autocert_core
{

CollisionChecker::CollisionChecker(
  std::shared_ptr<planning_scene::PlanningScene> planning_scene,
  const std::string& group_name)
: planning_scene_(planning_scene),
  group_name_(group_name)
{
  robot_state_ = std::make_unique<moveit::core::RobotState>(
    planning_scene_->getRobotModel());
  joint_model_group_ = planning_scene_->getRobotModel()->getJointModelGroup(group_name);
}

bool CollisionChecker::checkState(const std::vector<double>& joint_positions)
{
  robot_state_->setJointGroupPositions(joint_model_group_, joint_positions);
  robot_state_->update();
  
  return !planning_scene_->isStateColliding(*robot_state_, group_name_);
}

std::vector<bool> CollisionChecker::batchCheck(
  const std::vector<std::vector<double>>& joint_samples)
{
  std::vector<bool> results;
  results.reserve(joint_samples.size());
  
  for (const auto& sample : joint_samples)
  {
    results.push_back(checkState(sample));
  }
  
  return results;
}

} // namespace autocert_core

===== FILE: ./autocert_core/include/autocert_core/collision_checker.hpp =====
#ifndef AUTOCERT_CORE__COLLISION_CHECKER_HPP_
#define AUTOCERT_CORE__COLLISION_CHECKER_HPP_

#include <moveit/planning_scene/planning_scene.h>
#include <vector>
#include <string>
#include <memory>

namespace autocert_core
{

/**
 * @brief Collision checking utility for workspace sampling
 */
class CollisionChecker
{
public:
  /**
   * @brief Constructor
   * @param planning_scene MoveIt planning scene
   * @param group_name Planning group name
   */
  explicit CollisionChecker(
    std::shared_ptr<planning_scene::PlanningScene> planning_scene,
    const std::string& group_name);

  /**
   * @brief Check collision for a single state
   * @param joint_positions Joint configuration to check
   * @return True if collision-free
   */
  bool checkState(const std::vector<double>& joint_positions);

  /**
   * @brief Batch collision check
   * @param joint_samples Vector of joint configurations
   * @return Vector of boolean validity flags
   */
  std::vector<bool> batchCheck(const std::vector<std::vector<double>>& joint_samples);

private:
  std::shared_ptr<planning_scene::PlanningScene> planning_scene_;
  std::unique_ptr<moveit::core::RobotState> robot_state_;
  const moveit::core::JointModelGroup* joint_model_group_;
  std::string group_name_;
};

} // namespace autocert_core

#endif // AUTOCERT_CORE__COLLISION_CHECKER_HPP_

===== FILE: ./autocert_core/include/autocert_core/workspace_sampler.hpp =====
#pragma once

#include <rclcpp/rclcpp.hpp>
#include <moveit/robot_model_loader/robot_model_loader.hpp>
#include <moveit/robot_model/robot_model.hpp>
#include <moveit/robot_state/robot_state.hpp>
#include <moveit/planning_scene/planning_scene.hpp>
#include <geometry_msgs/msg/pose.hpp>
#include <mutex>
#include <atomic>
#include <thread>
#include <vector>
#include <memory>

namespace autocert_core
{

struct RobotInfo
{
  std::string robot_name;
  std::string planning_group;
  std::string end_effector_link;
  std::vector<std::string> joint_names;
  std::vector<std::string> link_names;
  std::vector<std::string> group_names;
  std::vector<double> joint_min_limits;
  std::vector<double> joint_max_limits;
  std::vector<double> joint_velocity_limits;
  size_t num_joints;
  size_t num_links;
};

struct BatchFKResult
{
  std::vector<geometry_msgs::msg::Pose> poses;
  std::vector<int> valid_indices;
  double reachability_index;
  double computation_time_ms;
};

class WorkspaceSampler
{
public:
  // Constructor takes node pointer and robot_description parameter NAME
  explicit WorkspaceSampler(
    const rclcpp::Node::SharedPtr& node,
    const std::string& robot_description_param);
  
  ~WorkspaceSampler();

  // Set the active planning group
  void setPlanningGroup(const std::string& group_name);
  
  // Set end effector link (optional)
  void setEndEffectorLink(const std::string& link_name);
  
  // Enable/disable collision checking
  void setCollisionChecking(bool enable);
  
  // Get robot information
  RobotInfo getRobotInfo() const;
  
  // Get joint limits as (min, max) pair
  std::pair<std::vector<double>, std::vector<double>> getJointLimits() const;
  
  // Get end effector link name
  std::string getEndEffectorLink() const { return end_effector_link_; }
  
  // Single FK computation (thread-safe)
  geometry_msgs::msg::Pose computeFK(const std::vector<double>& joint_values);
  
  // Batch FK computation (thread-safe)
  BatchFKResult computeBatchFK(
    const std::vector<std::vector<double>>& joint_samples,
    bool filter_collisions);
  
  // Check if a state is valid (thread-safe)
  bool isStateValid(const std::vector<double>& joint_values);

private:
  // Thread-local data structure
  struct ThreadLocalData
  {
    std::unique_ptr<moveit::core::RobotState> robot_state;
    planning_scene::PlanningScenePtr planning_scene;
    collision_detection::CollisionRequest collision_request;
    collision_detection::CollisionResult collision_result;
    uint64_t version;
  };
  
  // Get or create thread-local data
  ThreadLocalData* getThreadLocalData();
  
  // Helper to find default end effector from group
  std::string findDefaultEndEffector() const;
  
  // Initialize joint limits
  void initializeJointLimits();

  // Node pointer
  rclcpp::Node::SharedPtr node_;
  
  // Robot model (shared across threads - read-only)
  moveit::core::RobotModelConstPtr robot_model_;
  
  // Robot model loader
  std::shared_ptr<robot_model_loader::RobotModelLoader> model_loader_;
  
  // Base planning scene (for cloning - thread-safe)
  planning_scene::PlanningSceneConstPtr base_planning_scene_;
  
  // Active planning group
  const moveit::core::JointModelGroup* joint_model_group_;
  
  // Joint limits
  std::vector<double> joint_min_limits_;
  std::vector<double> joint_max_limits_;
  std::vector<double> joint_velocity_limits_;
  std::vector<std::string> joint_names_;
  
  // End effector link
  std::string end_effector_link_;
  
  // Planning group name
  std::string planning_group_;
  
  // Collision checking flag
  bool collision_checking_enabled_;
  
  // Version counter for tracking planning group changes
  std::atomic<uint64_t> state_version_{0};
  
  // Mutex for operations that modify shared state
  mutable std::mutex mutex_;
  
  // Robot info cache
  mutable RobotInfo cached_info_;
  mutable bool info_cached_{false};
};

} // namespace autocert_core

# Test identification
int32 pose_id          # Pose identifier (1-5 for ISO test)
int32 repetition       # Repetition number (1-30)
string pose_label      # Optional label (e.g., "P1", "CENTER")

# Commanded pose (from robot controller)
geometry_msgs/Pose commanded_pose

# Measured pose (from external measurement system)
geometry_msgs/Pose measured_pose

# Measurement metadata
builtin_interfaces/Time timestamp
string measurement_system   # e.g., "laser_tracker", "motion_capture"
string measurement_frame    # Frame ID of measurement
float64 measurement_quality # Quality metric (0-1)
